so this is technically from the find-commas script, but it's this:
make find-commas -- --max-n2d3p9 1259 --max-2-3-free-sopfr 127 --max-2-3-free-copfr 9999 --max-prime-limit 127 --upper-bound 56.8425030289c
so the idea was to just try to get basically the top N2D3P9 2,3-free classes up to 1259 (previously went as high as 307)
only constraint being that SoPF>3 of 127...
and this just doing a ton of duplication w/r/t each 2,3-free class, including every comma-sized thing, rather than just the LATE or LAAS comma for each 2,3-free class
